15:28:18  #
15:28:18  # Jenkins params override script to demonstrate excluding default
15:28:18  # notebooks and on-the-fly DEFAULT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_SCRIPT_URL file creation.
15:28:18  #
15:28:18  # This script is intended for param DEFAULT_CONFIG_PARAMETERS_SCRIPT_URL.
15:28:18  
15:28:18  # Scenario: we want to exclude some default notebooks that is known to not work
15:28:18  # or we do not need to generate the output at the end.
15:28:18  
15:28:18  # Create DEFAULT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_SCRIPT_URL file on-the-fly to run the notebooks
15:28:18  # from our external repo.
15:28:18  
15:28:18  DEFAULT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_SCRIPT_URL="/tmp/default-config-override.include.sh"
15:28:18  
15:28:18  # Need to export so it is visible in 'runtest'.
15:28:18  export DEFAULT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_SCRIPT_URL
15:28:18  
15:28:18  # Populate the content of our DEFAULT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_SCRIPT_URL.
15:28:18  echo '
15:28:18  #!/bin/sh
15:28:18  # Config override script to exclude default notebooks.
15:28:18  
15:28:18  #BLACKLIST_NOTEBOOKS="$PAVICS_SDI_DIR/docs/source/notebooks/esgf-dap.ipynb"
15:28:18  BLACKLIST_NOTEBOOKS=""
15:28:18  
15:28:18  if [ -n "$BLACKLIST_NOTEBOOKS" ]; then
15:28:18      sed_args=""
15:28:18      for bad_nb in $BLACKLIST_NOTEBOOKS; do
15:28:18          sed_args="$sed_args -e s@$bad_nb@@"
15:28:18      done
15:28:18  
15:28:18      NEW_NB_LIST="$(echo $NOTEBOOKS | sed $sed_args)"
15:28:18      NOTEBOOKS="$NEW_NB_LIST"
15:28:18  fi
15:28:18  
15:28:18  
15:28:18  # Select which notebooks to blacklist from generating output.
15:28:18  enable_resulting_nb() {
15:28:18      if [ x"$1" = x"$PAVICS_SDI_DIR/docs/source/notebooks/FAQ_dask_parallel.ipynb" ] ||
15:28:18         [ x"$1" = x"$PAVICS_LANDING_DIR/content/notebooks/climate_indicators/PAVICStutorial_ClimateDataAnalysis-3Climate-Indicators.ipynb" ]; then
15:28:18          # Blacklist those notebooks.
15:28:18          echo "Skipping \"$1\"."
15:28:18          return 1
15:28:18      else
15:28:18          # Enable all the rest.
15:28:18          return 0
15:28:18      fi
15:28:18  }
